\
Welcome to Persian Gulf at War!\
\
Please take a moment to read the briefing once you select a slot\, it  contains critical information regarding supplies at airbases and mission objectives.  If you cannot spawn in a certain slot it's probably because there are not any of that aircraft available at the airfield at that time.  Al Dhafra will ALWAYS have unlimited aircraft.\
\
Iranian forces have stormed across the Strait of Hormuz\, both closing the Strait to shipping traffic and occupying Oman and parts of UAE.  After an international outcry\, a coalition including the United States\, France\, Sweden\, and additional nations formed and has been steadily resupplying existing allied bases in the region in preparation of armed intervention.\
\
MAGIC_IFF\
\
ATIS Al Dhafra AFB 249.000\
\
OverlordBot provides ATC and AWACS functionality over SRS\
See https://gitlab.com/overlord-bot/srs-bot/-/wikis/Interaction for instructions on how to use this bot and supported radio calls. See briefing for frequencies\
\
